Require Import UniMath.Foundations.PartD.

Require Import UniMath.MoreFoundations.Tactics.

Require Import UniMath.CategoryTheory.Core.Categories.
Require Import UniMath.CategoryTheory.Core.Functors.
Require Import UniMath.CategoryTheory.Core.NaturalTransformations.
Require Import UniMath.CategoryTheory.FunctorCategory.
Require Import UniMath.CategoryTheory.whiskering.

Require Import UniMath.CategoryTheory.Limits.Terminal.
Require Import UniMath.CategoryTheory.FunctorAlgebras.
Require Import UniMath.CategoryTheory.PointedFunctors.
Require Import UniMath.SubstitutionSystems.Signatures.
Require Import UniMath.CategoryTheory.BicatOfCatsElementary.
Require Import UniMath.SubstitutionSystems.Notation.

Local Open Scope subsys.

Require Import UniMath.CategoryTheory.PointedFunctorsComposition.

Local Open Scope cat.

Section around_δ.

Context (C : category).

(* G^n+1 *)
Fixpoint iter_functor1 (G: functor C C) (n : nat) : functor C C := match n with
  | O => G
  | S n' => functor_composite (iter_functor1 G n') G
  end.

(** The category of pointed endofunctors on [C] *)
Local Notation "'Ptd'" := (category_Ptd C).
(** The category of endofunctors on [C] *)
Local Notation "'EndC'":= ([C, C]) .

(** distributivity with laws as a simple form the strength with laws,
    for endofunctors on the base category

    in July 2023, it became clear that this should rather have been
    called a pointed lax commutator; since a paper is based on this
    notion, we keep the name
*)
Section def_of_δ.

Context (G : EndC).

Definition δ_source : functor Ptd EndC :=
  functor_compose (functor_ptd_forget C) (post_comp_functor G).

Definition δ_target : functor Ptd EndC :=
  functor_compose (functor_ptd_forget C) (pre_comp_functor G).

Section δ_laws.

Context (δ : δ_source ⟹ δ_target).

(* Should be ρ_G^-1 ∘ λ_G ? *)
Definition δ_law1 : UU := δ (id_Ptd C) = identity G.
Let D' Ze Ze' :=
  nat_trans_comp (rassociator_CAT (pr1 Ze) (pr1 Ze') G)
 (nat_trans_comp (lwhisker_CAT (pr1 Ze) (δ Ze'))
 (nat_trans_comp (lassociator_CAT (pr1 Ze) G (pr1 Ze'))
 (nat_trans_comp (rwhisker_CAT (pr1 Ze') (δ Ze))
                 (rassociator_CAT G (pr1 Ze) (pr1 Ze'))))).
Definition δ_law2 : UU := ∏ Ze Ze', δ (Ze p• Ze') = D' Ze Ze'.

(** the following variant is more suitable for communication about the results *)
Definition δ_law2_nicer : UU := ∏ Ze Ze',
    δ (Ze p• Ze') =
      # (pre_comp_functor (pr1 Ze)) (δ Ze') · # (post_comp_functor (pr1 Ze')) (δ Ze).


C: category
G: [C, C]
δ: δ_source ⟹ δ_target
D':= λ Ze Ze' : ∑ F : C ⟶ C, functor_identity C ⟹ F,
nat_trans_comp
  (rassociator_CAT (pr1 Ze) (pr1 Ze') G)
  (nat_trans_comp (lwhisker_CAT (pr1 Ze) (δ Ze'))
     (nat_trans_comp
        (lassociator_CAT (pr1 Ze) G (pr1 Ze'))
        (nat_trans_comp
           (rwhisker_CAT (pr1 Ze') (δ Ze))
           (rassociator_CAT G (pr1 Ze) (pr1 Ze'))))): ∏ Ze Ze' : ∑ F : C ⟶ C, functor_identity C ⟹ F,
functor_compose
  (functor_compose (pr1 Ze) (pr1 Ze')) G
⟹ functor_compose G
    (functor_compose (pr1 Ze) (pr1 Ze'))
δ_law2 → δ_law2_nicer


C: category
G: [C, C]
δ: δ_source ⟹ δ_target
D':= λ Ze Ze' : ∑ F : C ⟶ C, functor_identity C ⟹ F,
nat_trans_comp
  (rassociator_CAT (pr1 Ze) (pr1 Ze') G)

functor_compose
  (functor_compose (pr1 Ze) (pr1 Ze')) G
⟹ functor_compose G
    (functor_compose (pr1 Ze) (pr1 Ze'))
δ_law2 → δ_law2_nicer

  (rassociator_CAT (pr1 Ze) (pr1 Ze') G)

  (functor_compose (pr1 Ze) (pr1 Ze')) G

    (functor_compose (pr1 Ze) (pr1 Ze'))
Hyp: δ_law2
Ze, Ze': ptd_obj C
Hypinst: δ (Ze p• Ze') = D' Ze Ze'
c: C
identity (G (pr1 Ze' (pr1 Ze c)))
· (pr1 (δ Ze') (pr1 (pr1 Ze) c)
   · (identity (pr1 Ze' (G (pr1 Ze c)))
      · (# (pr1 (pr1 Ze')) (pr1 (δ Ze) c)
         · identity (pr1 Ze' (pr1 Ze (G c)))))) =
pr1 (δ Ze') (pr1 (pr1 Ze) c)
· # (pr1 (pr1 Ze')) (pr1 (δ Ze) c)

    (functor_compose (pr1 Ze) (pr1 Ze'))
Hyp: δ_law2
Ze, Ze': ptd_obj C
Hypinst: δ (Ze p• Ze') = D' Ze Ze'
c: C
pr1 (δ Ze') (pr1 (pr1 Ze) c)
· (# (pr1 (pr1 Ze')) (pr1 (δ Ze) c)
   · identity (pr1 Ze' (pr1 Ze (G c)))) =
pr1 (δ Ze') (pr1 (pr1 Ze) c)
· # (pr1 (pr1 Ze')) (pr1 (δ Ze) c)

· # (pr1 (pr1 Ze')) (pr1 (δ Ze) c)

  apply idpath.
Qed.

    (functor_compose (pr1 Ze) (pr1 Ze'))

End δ_laws.

Definition DistributiveLaw : UU := ∑ δ : δ_source ⟹ δ_target, δ_law1 δ × δ_law2 δ.

Definition δ (DL : DistributiveLaw) : δ_source ⟹ δ_target := pr1 DL.

Definition distributive_law1 (DL : DistributiveLaw) : δ_law1 _ := pr1 (pr2 DL).

Definition distributive_law2 (DL : DistributiveLaw) : δ_law2 _ := pr2 (pr2 DL).

End def_of_δ.

         (functor_composite_data (ptd_forget_data C)
            (pre_composition_functor_data C C C
               (functor_identity C))) t)
        (((λ x : ptd_ob_mor C,
           ((λ y : C,
             identity (pr1 x y)
             :
             C
             ⟦ functor_composite_data
                 (ptd_forget_data C)
                 (post_composition_functor_data C C C
                    (functor_identity C)) x y,
             functor_composite_data
               (ptd_forget_data C)
               (pre_composition_functor_data C C C
                  (functor_identity C)) x y ⟧)
            :
            nat_trans_data
              (functor_composite_data
                 (ptd_forget_data C)
                 (post_composition_functor_data C C C
                    (functor_identity C)) x)
              (functor_composite_data
                 (ptd_forget_data C)
                 (pre_composition_functor_data C C C
                    (functor_identity C)) x)),,
           DL_id_subproof x)
          :
          nat_trans_data
            (functor_composite_data
               (ptd_forget_data C)
               (post_composition_functor_data C C C
                  (functor_identity C)))
            (functor_composite_data
               (ptd_forget_data C)
               (pre_composition_functor_data C C C
                  (functor_identity C))))
         :
         nat_trans_data
           (functor_composite_data (ptd_forget_data C)
              (post_composition_functor_data C C C
                 (functor_identity C)))
           (functor_composite_data (ptd_forget_data C)
              (pre_composition_functor_data C C C
                 (functor_identity C))))))
 
C: category
δ_law1 (functor_identity C)
  ((λ x : ptd_ob_mor C,
    (λ y : C, identity (pr1 x y)),, DL_id_subproof x),,
   DL_id_subproof0)
C: category
δ_law2 (functor_identity C)
  ((λ x : ptd_ob_mor C,
    (λ y : C, identity (pr1 x y)),, DL_id_subproof x),,
   DL_id_subproof0)

  
C: category
δ_law1 (functor_identity C)
  ((λ x : ptd_ob_mor C,
    (λ y : C, identity (pr1 x y)),, DL_id_subproof x),,
   DL_id_subproof0)
 apply nat_trans_eq_alt; intro c; simpl; apply idpath.
  
C: category
δ_law2 (functor_identity C)
  ((λ x : ptd_ob_mor C,
    (λ y : C, identity (pr1 x y)),, DL_id_subproof x),,
   DL_id_subproof0)
 
C: category
Ze, Ze': ptd_obj C
c: C
identity (pr1 Ze' (pr1 Ze c)) =
identity (pr1 Ze' (pr1 Ze c))
· (identity (pr1 Ze' (pr1 (pr1 Ze) c))
   · (identity (pr1 Ze' (pr1 Ze c))
      · (# (pr1 (pr1 Ze')) (identity (pr1 Ze c))
         · identity (pr1 Ze' (pr1 Ze c)))))
 
C: category
Ze, Ze': ptd_obj C
c: C
identity (pr1 Ze' (pr1 Ze c)) =
# (pr1 (pr1 Ze')) (identity (pr1 Ze c))
· identity (pr1 Ze' (pr1 Ze c))

    
C: category
Ze, Ze': ptd_obj C
c: C
identity (pr1 Ze' (pr1 Ze c)) =
# (pr1 (pr1 Ze')) (identity (pr1 Ze c))
 
C: category
Ze, Ze': ptd_obj C
c: C
# (pr1 (pr1 Ze')) (identity (pr1 Ze c)) =
identity (pr1 Ze' (pr1 Ze c))
 apply functor_id.
Defined.

End δ_for_id.

(** Construct θ in a Signature in the case when the functor is
    precomposition with a functor G from a family of simpler
    distributive laws δ *)
Section θ_from_δ.

Context (G : functor C C) (DL : DistributiveLaw G).

Let precompG := (pre_composition_functor _ C C G).

(** See Lemma 11 of "From Signatures to Monads in UniMath" in Ahrens, Matthes and Mörtberg *)

⟧

⟧

  exact (F3 · (F2 · F1)).
Defined.

· # (pr1 F2) (pr1 (δ G DL Ze2) c) =

  apply pathsinv0, nat_trans_ax.
Qed.

Definition θ_from_δ : PrestrengthForSignature precompG := tpair _ _ is_nat_trans_θ_from_δ_mor.

· (pr1 (pr1 DL Ze') (pr1 (pr1 Ze) c)
   · (identity (pr1 Ze' (G (pr1 Ze c)))
      · (# (pr1 (pr1 Ze')) (pr1 (pr1 DL Ze) c)
         · identity (pr1 Ze' (pr1 Ze (G c))))))
→ identity (F (G (pr1 Ze' (pr1 Ze c))))
  · (# (pr1 F) (pr1 (δ G DL (Ze p• Ze')) c)
     · identity (F (pr1 Ze' (pr1 Ze (G c)))))
  · identity (F (Z' (Z (pr1 G c)))) =
  identity (F (G (Z' (Z c))))
  · (identity (F (G (pr1 Ze' (pr1 Z c))))
     · (# (pr1 F) (pr1 (δ G DL Ze') (pr1 Z c))
        · identity (F (pr1 Ze' (G (pr1 Z c))))))

     · (# F (# Z' (pr1 (δ G DL Ze) c))
        · identity (F (Z' (pr1 Ze (G c))))))

c: C
H: pr1 DL (Ze p• Ze') c =

· # F (# Z' (pr1 (δ G DL Ze) c))

  apply functor_comp.
Qed.

· pr1 (δ G2 DL2 Ze') (pr1 G1 (pr1 (pr1 Ze) c))
· # (pr1 (pr1 Ze'))
    (# (pr1 G2) (pr1 (δ G1 DL1 Ze) c)
     · pr1 (δ G2 DL2 Ze) (pr1 G1 c))

δ_genoption ((Z,, e) p• (Z',, e')) =
nat_trans_comp
  (rassociator_CAT (pr1 (Z,, e)) (pr1 (Z',, e'))
     genopt)
  (nat_trans_comp
     (lwhisker_CAT (pr1 (Z,, e))
        (δ_genoption (Z',, e')))
     (nat_trans_comp
        (lassociator_CAT (pr1 (Z,, e)) genopt
           (pr1 (Z',, e')))
        (nat_trans_comp
           (rwhisker_CAT (pr1 (Z',, e'))
              (δ_genoption (Z,, e)))
           (rassociator_CAT genopt (pr1 (Z,, e))
              (pr1 (Z',, e'))))))

identity
  (BinCoproduct_of_functors_ob C C CC
     (constant_functor C C A) (functor_identity C)
     (Z' (Z c)))
· (δ_genoption_mor (Z',, e') (pr1 Z c)
   · (identity
        (Z'
           (BinCoproduct_of_functors_ob C C CC
              (constant_functor C C A)
              (functor_identity C) (Z c)))
      · (# (pr1 Z') (δ_genoption_mor (Z,, e) c)
         · identity
             (Z'
                (Z
                   (BinCoproduct_of_functors_ob C C CC
                      (constant_functor C C A)
                      (functor_identity C) c))))))

  
C: category
A: C
CC: BinCoproducts C
genopt:= constcoprod_functor1 CC A: C ⟶ C
Z: C ⟶ C
e: functor_identity C ⟹ Z
Z': C ⟶ C
e': functor_identity C ⟹ Z'
c: C
BinCoproductArrow (CC A (Z' (Z c)))
  (BinCoproductIn1 (CC A c)
   · (pr1 e (CC A c) · pr1 e' (pr1 Z (CC A c))))
  (# Z' (# Z (BinCoproductIn2 (CC A c)))) =
identity (CC A (Z' (Z c)))
· (BinCoproductArrow (CC A (Z' (pr1 Z c)))
     (BinCoproductIn1 (CC A (pr1 Z c))
      · e' (CC A (pr1 Z c)))
     (# Z' (BinCoproductIn2 (CC A (pr1 Z c))))
   · (identity (Z' (CC A (Z c)))
      · (# (pr1 Z')
           (BinCoproductArrow (CC A (Z c))
              (BinCoproductIn1 (CC A c) · e (CC A c))
              (# Z (BinCoproductIn2 (CC A c))))
         · identity (Z' (Z (CC A c))))))

Definition precomp_genoption_Signature : Signature C C C :=
  θ_from_δ_Signature genopt genoption_DistributiveLaw.

End genoption_sig.

(** trivially instantiate previous section to option functor *)
Section option_sig.

Context (TC : Terminal C) (CC : BinCoproducts C).

  Let opt := option_functor CC TC.

  Definition δ_option: δ_source opt ⟹ δ_target opt := δ_genoption TC CC.
  Definition δ_law1_option :=  δ_law1_genoption TC CC.
  Definition δ_law2_option :=  δ_law2_genoption TC CC.
  Definition option_DistributiveLaw : DistributiveLaw opt := genoption_DistributiveLaw TC CC.
  Definition precomp_option_Signature : Signature C C C := precomp_genoption_Signature TC CC.

End option_sig.

DL: DistributiveLaw G
n: nat
IHn: DistributiveLaw (iter_functor1 G n)
DistributiveLaw
  ((fix iter_functor1
      (G : C ⟶ C) (n : nat) {struct n} : C ⟶ C :=
      match n with
      | 0 => G
      | S n' => iter_functor1 G n' ∙ G
      end) G n)
 apply IHn.
    
C: category
G: C ⟶ C
DL: DistributiveLaw G
n: nat
IHn: DistributiveLaw (iter_functor1 G n)
DistributiveLaw G
 exact DL.
Defined.

End iter1_dl.

End around_δ.

Defined.

(** Signature for the Id functor *)
Definition IdSignature : Signature C D D := tpair _ (functor_identity _) θ_functor_identity.
(** an alternative approach would be to go through θ_from_δ_Signature, based on the
observation that functor_identity [C,C,hsC] and
pre_comp_functor hsC hsC (functor_identity C) are isomorphic;
however, they are probably not propositionally equal, and so the benefit is marginal *)

End id_signature.

 now split; intros x; intros; apply (nat_trans_eq (homset_property D)); intro c; simpl; rewrite !id_left.
Defined.

Definition ConstConstSignature : Signature C D D' := tpair _ H θ_const_const.

End constantly_constant_signature.

(** Transform a signature with strength θ with underlying functor H into
    a signature with strength Gθ for the functor that comes from
    post-composition of all HX with a functor G
    G need not be an endofunctor, which is why the strength concept had
    to be given more heterogeneously than only on endofunctors on
    endofunctor categories
 *)
Section θ_for_postcomposition.

Context (C D D' E : category).

(** The category of pointed endofunctors on [C] *)
Local Notation "'Ptd'" := (category_Ptd C).
(** The category of endofunctors on [C] *)
Local Notation "'EndC'":= ([C, C]) .

Context (S: Signature C D D').

Let H : functor [C, D'] [C, D] := Signature_Functor S.
Let θ : nat_trans (θ_source H) (θ_target H) := theta S.
Let θ_strength1 := Sig_strength_law1 S.
Let θ_strength2 := Sig_strength_law2 S.
Context (G : [D, E]).

Let GH : functor [C, D'] [C, E] := functor_composite H (post_comp_functor G).


C, D, D', E: category
S: Signature C D D'
H:= S: [C, D'] ⟶ [C, D]
θ:= theta S: θ_source H ⟹ θ_target H
θ_strength1:= Sig_strength_law1 S: θ_Strength1_int (pr1 (pr2 S))
θ_strength2:= Sig_strength_law2 S: θ_Strength2_int (pr1 (pr2 S))
G: [D, E]
GH:= H ∙ post_comp_functor G: [C, D'] ⟶ [C, E]
XZe: [C, D'] ⊠ Ptd
[C, E] ⟦ θ_source GH XZe, θ_target GH XZe ⟧

G: [D, E]
GH:= H ∙ post_comp_functor G: [C, D'] ⟶ [C, E]
XZe: [C, D'] ⊠ Ptd
X:= pr1 XZe: [C, D']
Z:= pr1 (pr2 XZe) : [C, C]: [C, C]
F1:= lassociator_CAT Z (H X) G: [C, E]
⟦ functor_compose Z (functor_compose (H X) G),
functor_compose (functor_compose Z (H X)) G ⟧
[C, E] ⟦ θ_source GH XZe, θ_target GH XZe ⟧

  
C, D, D', E: category
S: Signature C D D'
H:= S: [C, D'] ⟶ [C, D]
θ:= theta S: θ_source H ⟹ θ_target H
θ_strength1:= Sig_strength_law1 S: θ_Strength1_int (pr1 (pr2 S))
θ_strength2:= Sig_strength_law2 S: θ_Strength2_int (pr1 (pr2 S))
G: [D, E]
GH:= H ∙ post_comp_functor G: [C, D'] ⟶ [C, E]
XZe: [C, D'] ⊠ Ptd
X:= pr1 XZe: [C, D']
Z:= pr1 (pr2 XZe) : [C, C]: [C, C]
F1:= lassociator_CAT Z (H X) G: [C, E]
⟦ functor_compose Z (functor_compose (H X) G),
functor_compose (functor_compose Z (H X)) G ⟧
F2:= rwhisker_CAT G (θ XZe): [C, E] ⟦ functor_compose (θ_source H XZe) G,
functor_compose (θ_target H XZe) G ⟧
[C, E] ⟦ θ_source GH XZe, θ_target GH XZe ⟧

  exact (F1 · F2).
Defined.

c: C

· # (pr1 G) (pr1 (# H (pr1 αX)) (pr1 (pr1 X2) c))
· (identity (G (H F2 (pr1 X2 c)))
   · # (pr1 G) (pr1 (θ (F2,, X2)) c)) =

· # (pr1 G) (pr1 (θ (F1,, X1)) c)

    (pr1

             (pr1 (pr2 αX)) F1
           · pre_whisker_in_funcat C C D' (pr1 X2)
               (pr1 αX))) c)

# (pr1 G) (pr1 (θ (F ⊗ Ze')) (pr1 (pr1 Ze) c))
· # (pr1 G)
    (pr1 (θ (functor_compose (pr1 Ze') F ⊗ Ze)) c)

θ_strength1:= Sig_strength_law1 S: θ_Strength1_int (pr1 (pr2 S))

C, D, D', E: category
S: Signature C D D'
H:= S: [C, D'] ⟶ [C, D]
θ:= theta S: θ_source H ⟹ θ_target H
θ_strength1:= Sig_strength_law1 S: θ_Strength1_int (pr1 (pr2 S))
θ_strength2:= Sig_strength_law2 S: θ_Strength2_int (pr1 (pr2 S))
G: [D, E]
GH:= H ∙ post_comp_functor G: [C, D'] ⟶ [C, E]
F: [C, D']
Ze, Ze': Ptd
Z:= pr1 Ze: C ⟶ C
Z':= pr1 Ze': C ⟶ C
c: C
pr1 (pr2 S) (F ⊗ Ze p• Ze') c
· # (pr1 S) (rassociator_CAT (pr1 Ze) (pr1 Ze') F) c =
identity (pr1 S F (pr1 Ze' (pr1 Ze c)))
· pr1 (pr1 (pr2 S) (F ⊗ Ze')) (pr1 (pr1 Ze) c)
· pr1 (pr2 S) (functor_compose (pr1 Ze') F ⊗ Ze) c
→ pr1 (θ (F ⊗ Ze')) (pr1 (pr1 Ze) c)
  · pr1 (θ (functor_compose (pr1 Ze') F ⊗ Ze)) c =
  pr1 (θ (F ⊗ Ze p• Ze')) c
  · pr1 (# H (rassociator_CAT (pr1 Ze) (pr1 Ze') F)) c

  
C, D, D', E: category
S: Signature C D D'
H:= S: [C, D'] ⟶ [C, D]
θ:= theta S: θ_source H ⟹ θ_target H
θ_strength1:= Sig_strength_law1 S: θ_Strength1_int (pr1 (pr2 S))
θ_strength2:= Sig_strength_law2 S: θ_Strength2_int (pr1 (pr2 S))
G: [D, E]
GH:= H ∙ post_comp_functor G: [C, D'] ⟶ [C, E]
F: [C, D']
Ze, Ze': Ptd
Z:= pr1 Ze: C ⟶ C
Z':= pr1 Ze': C ⟶ C
c: C
pr1 (pr2 S) (F ⊗ Ze p• Ze') c
· # (pr1 S) (rassociator_CAT (pr1 Ze) (pr1 Ze') F) c =
pr1 (pr1 (pr2 S) (F ⊗ Ze')) (pr1 (pr1 Ze) c)
· pr1 (pr2 S) (functor_compose (pr1 Ze') F ⊗ Ze) c
→ pr1 (θ (F ⊗ Ze')) (pr1 (pr1 Ze) c)
  · pr1 (θ (functor_compose (pr1 Ze') F ⊗ Ze)) c =
  pr1 (θ (F ⊗ Ze p• Ze')) c
  · pr1 (# H (rassociator_CAT (pr1 Ze) (pr1 Ze') F)) c

  
C, D, D', E: category
S: Signature C D D'
H:= S: [C, D'] ⟶ [C, D]
θ:= theta S: θ_source H ⟹ θ_target H
θ_strength1:= Sig_strength_law1 S: θ_Strength1_int (pr1 (pr2 S))
θ_strength2:= Sig_strength_law2 S: θ_Strength2_int (pr1 (pr2 S))
G: [D, E]
GH:= H ∙ post_comp_functor G: [C, D'] ⟶ [C, E]
F: [C, D']
Ze, Ze': Ptd
Z:= pr1 Ze: C ⟶ C
Z':= pr1 Ze': C ⟶ C
c: C
Hyp: pr1 (pr2 S) (F ⊗ Ze p• Ze') c
· # (pr1 S)
    (rassociator_CAT (pr1 Ze) (pr1 Ze') F) c =
pr1 (pr1 (pr2 S) (F ⊗ Ze')) (pr1 (pr1 Ze) c)
· pr1 (pr2 S) (functor_compose (pr1 Ze') F ⊗ Ze)
    c
pr1 (θ (F ⊗ Ze')) (pr1 (pr1 Ze) c)
· pr1 (θ (functor_compose (pr1 Ze') F ⊗ Ze)) c =
pr1 (θ (F ⊗ Ze p• Ze')) c
· pr1 (# H (rassociator_CAT (pr1 Ze) (pr1 Ze') F)) c

  apply pathsinv0, Hyp.
Qed.

Definition Gθ_with_laws : StrengthForSignature GH := tpair _ Gθ (Gθ_Strength1_int ,, Gθ_Strength2_int).

Definition Gθ_Signature : Signature C E D' := tpair _ GH Gθ_with_laws.

End θ_for_postcomposition.
